<username>Robert Peacock<//username><Gmap_id>0x80dceeecddcecfa3:0x9056e5ed8d52ab23</Gmap_id><Pictures>None< /Pictures><Resp>None</Resp><time>1422728811447< /time>< Rating>
1</Rating>
< text>
As noted by others, Camden often encourages residents to write reviews in order to win prizes. While I have no intention of entering such raffles I thought I would still provide my insight.

After living here for 15 months I just recently renewed my lease. My rent increased by 10% and if it wasn't for the convenience of being able to walk to work from the complex I would have relocated. Rental quotes also fluctuate, sometimes by hundreds of dollars, on the website, so be careful when doing your research online.

The resident information number directs you to a call center and on several occasions I have been given contradicting information from the representatives. For instance, I was told that as long as my parking permit was displayed I could park in a spot for an extended period of time. The following day a leasing representative sent an email to the complex with parking reminders stating "The maximum amount of time to be parked in one resident spot is 72 hours."

Parking: While parking is by permit only there are no assigned spots, so finding a place to park your car after work or during the weekend is often impossible and requires parking in one of the other buildings. As I said above, residents are only able to park in the same spot for 72 hours or their car will be towed, so hopefully you have a friend or family member willing to move your car if your are taking any more than a 3 day vacation. Visitor parking is always nearly impossible to find.

Technology package: There is a mandatory "technology package" that is not included in the price of your rent. It is an additional $62 per month and only includes expanded, non-HD, cable. This price is not negotiable, even if you sign up for additional cable or internet though COX.

Plumbing: Within the first year of living in my apartment I had three separate water leaks. One required filing an insurance claim (which thankfully Camden requires you to have,) and all three required multiple days of a dehumidifier running 24/7 to dry out the unit before the drywall or cabinets could be replaced.

Trash fee: The trash fee is based on the size of the unit, not occupancy. So a family of three or four pays the same amount as a family of one living in a comparably sized unit.

Overall the renovated apartments have an inviting, upscale look but do not make up for the larger issues plaguing the complex.</text>

< review>
After reading reviews that touted Ledgers' big selection, I was excited to add to my Scotch collection during a visit to this place. However, it did not live up to its reputation at all. It took a while to get someone's attention, and when I did I let him know I was looking to add a few uncommon bottles. I was prepared to spend a lot of money, excited about finding some new bottles. When I asked him for a specific brand, he showed me where it was and there was only one bottle, the most basic variety. I was confused, because even some grocery stores have more than one variety of this brand. He then showed me a different corner of the store where there was another bottle. I then wandered around the store and found two other varieties in seemingly random locations. The entire time, I needed him to help me but he was busy helping a customer select lottery numbers. The impression I left with was that this is essentially a glorified corner deli that has quite a lot of bottles, but there is no real expertise or passion here. I ended up at Cask in Oakland instead, which has a decent selection, is better organized, and pays more attention to the customer.< /review>

< Text>
Excellent selection of hard to find spirits! They carry multiple overproof rums while most stores don't carry any. Most of the staff was very helpful finding the bottles I wanted. They stock checked when they couldn't find one and let me know when they're getting it back in stock without my having to ask for either. A lot of the spirits they carry are behind a counter, so you have to ask for someone to get you things. Unfortunately, the one person helping us didn't know their stock well, didn't acknowledge he didn't understand what I was asking for, and stood in front of the area we were searching blocking my view. Other than that, great experience. I'm excited to go back.< /Text>

<user_name>Luis Cruz< /user_name><Date>1458154967857< /Date><Rating>5< /Rating><review>Unfortunately, there is no rebuttal section on Google. So, I am left with commenting in the review section. Sorry folks. It's not a shameless plug, but more of a  global response to the  negative reviews that have been responded to on YELP and other sites.

Please take any review that is written for any business with a huge boulder of salt. Out of the many clients that a business sees in a week, month, and years, there will always be the less than 1% that will take to the public forums to vent very biased and often erroneous recounting of their experiences.  The problem with the latter is that a business owner is not allowed to provide their side of the story so the consumer can make an educated decision.  Please take all the above into account when you consider visiting a business.

We value our relationship with our clients and patients. They mean the world to us because taking care of them is our passion and life's mission. We ask that you take advantage of our promotional offers and decide for yourselves.

Sincerely,

American Veterinary Hospital, Inc.<//review><pics>None</pics><Resp>None<//Resp><Gmap_id>0x80e828528629d17d:0x38b1ba02d9b275a5< /Gmap_id></record></dataset><record>

< text>
We've been storing here now for a couple of years and the experience has been great.

- The location is close off the freeway (I-10) and is easy to get to.
- The facilities are clean and well maintained.
- The hallways and units are well lit and the access is very secure.

The team of people who work here are awesome.  The other day, we had to get our lock cut (lost key) and Bernadette was extremely helpful.  Although it was a tough round disk lock, she didn't give up and after 30 minutes, she was able to cut it off.

There are other Extra Space Storage locations throughout LA, but for the size and location, this one offers the best bang for your buck.  Similar units to ours, although they would be closer to where we live, are 35% to 45% more per month.

If you are looking for a storage unit central to Mid-City, Miracle Mile, USC or downtown, come down and talk to the gang at Extra-space Storage on Pico and Normandie.

Thanks!</text>
